Automatically classifies tasks into compliance tiers and enforces appropriate verification.\n\n**Key Benefits**:\n- Single command replaces confusion between `sc:task` and `sc:task-mcp`\n- Automatic tier classification with confidence scoring\n- Appropriate verification for each task type\n- Prevents over-engineering for trivial changes\n- Ensures safety for critical changes\n\n## Triggers\n\nUse `/sc:task` when:\n- Task involves code modifications with downstream impacts\n- Complexity score >0.6 with code modifications\n- Multi-file scope (>2 estimated affected files)\n- Security domain paths detected (auth/, security/, crypto/)\n- Refactoring or system-wide changes requested\n\n**Auto-Suggest Keywords**:\n- High confidence: \"implement feature\", \"refactor system\", \"fix security\", \"add authentication\", \"update database schema\"\n- Moderate confidence: \"add new\", \"create component\", \"update service\", \"modify API\"\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n/sc:task [description]                           # Auto-detect all dimensions\n/sc:task [description] --compliance strict       # Force STRICT tier\n/sc:task [description] --compliance light        # Force LIGHT tier\n/sc:task [description] --skip-compliance         # Bypass compliance (escape hatch)\n/sc:task [description] --verify auto             # Auto-select verification\n```\n\n## Behavioral Flow\n\n### 0. Classification (Already Performed)\n\nClassification was handled by the `/sc:task` command before this skill was invoked. The tier has been determined and the classification header has been emitted. This human-readable display is for user understanding.\n\n### 3. Execution Phase\n\nExecute task according to tier requirements:\n\n**STRICT Execution**:\n1. Activate project (mcp__serena__activate_project)\n2. Verify git working directory clean (git status)\n3. Load codebase context (codebase-retrieval)\n4. Check relevant memories (list_memories -> read_memory)\n5. Identify all affected files and test files\n6. Make changes with full checklist\n7. Identify all files that import changed code\n8. Load context via codebase-retrieval\n2. Search downstream impacts (find_referencing_symbols OR grep)\n3. Make changes\n4. Run affected tests OR document manual verification\n5. Verify basic functionality\n\n**LIGHT Execution**:\n1. Quick scope check (files/lines within bounds)\n2. Make changes\n3. Quick sanity check (syntax valid, no obvious errors)\n4. Proceed with judgment\n\n**EXEMPT Execution**:\n1. Execute immediately\n2. No verification overhead\n\n### 4. Verification Phase\n\nRoute to appropriate verification based on tier and paths:\n\n| Compliance Tier | Verification Method | Token Cost | Timeout |\n|-----------------|---------------------|------------|---------|\n| STRICT | Sub-agent (quality-engineer) | 3-5K | 60s |\n| STANDARD | Direct test execution | 300-500 | 30s |\n| LIGHT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n| EXEMPT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n\n**Critical Path Override**: Paths matching `auth/`, `security/`, `crypto/`, `models/`, `migrations/` always trigger CRITICAL verification regardless of compliance tier.\n\n**Trivial Path Override**: Paths matching `*.md`, `docs/`, `*test*.py` may skip verification.\n\n### 5. Feedback Collection\n\nAfter completion, collect implicit feedback:\n- Track if user overrode tier (implicit classification feedback)\n- Note smooth completion vs errors (quality signal)\n- Store for calibration learning\n\n## MCP Integration\n\n**Required Servers by Tier**:\n- STRICT: Sequential, Serena (fallback not allowed)\n- STANDARD: Sequential, Context7 (fallback allowed)\n- LIGHT: None required (fallback allowed)\n- EXEMPT: None required\n\n**Circuit Breaker Behavior**:\n- If required servers unavailable for STRICT tier, block task execution\n- For other tiers, use fallbacks with noted limitations\n\n## Tool Coordination\n\n**Planning Phase**:\n1. TodoWrite: Create task breakdown\n2. codebase-retrieval: Load context\n3. list_memories / read_memory: Check project state\n\n**Execution Phase**:\n1. Edit/MultiEdit/Write: Make changes\n2. Grep/Glob: Find references\n3. find_referencing_symbols: Trace dependencies\n\n**Verification Phase**:\n1. Task (quality-engineer): Spawn verification agent (STRICT only)\n2. Bash: Run tests directly (STANDARD)\n3. think_about_task_adherence: Reflect on completeness\n\n**Completion Phase**:\n1. write_memory: Save session state\n2. think_about_whether_you_are_done: Final check\n\n## Examples\n\n### STRICT Task\n```\n/sc:task \"implement user authentication with JWT\"\n\n-> Classified as STRICT (security domain, authentication keyword)\n-> Full 6-category checklist classification\n-> Full verification enforced\n```\n\n## Boundaries\n\n**Will:**\n- Classify tasks into appropriate compliance tiers\n- Enforce tier-appropriate verification requirements\n- Provide confidence scoring with rationale\n- Track feedback for continuous calibration\n- Support user overrides with justification\n\n**Will Not:**\n- Skip safety-critical verification for STRICT tasks\n- Measurement |\n|--------|--------|-------------|\n| Tier classification accuracy | >=80% | User feedback on appropriateness |\n| User confusion rate | <10% | \"Which command?\" questions eliminated deliverables\n    58→    source_deliverables = [\n    59→        d for d in deliverables\n    60→        if d.kind != DeliverableKind.INVARIANT_CHECK\n    61→    ]\n    62→\n    63→    # Step 1: Focus 107→\n   108→    # Step 7: Render section\n   109→    section = _render_registry_section(entries, generated)\n   110→\n   111→    return InvariantRegistryOutput(\n   112→        entries=entries,\n IntroductionType.SELF_ASSIGNMENT: f\"{var} is not None\",\n   133→        IntroductionType.REPLACEMENT: f\"{var} is not None\",\n   134→        IntroductionType.GENERIC: f\"{var} is not None\",\n   135→    }\n   136→    return type_predicates.get(detection.introduction_type, f\"{var} is not None\")\n   137→\n   138→\n   139→def _infer_scope(detection: DetectionResult) -> str:\n   140→    \"\"\"Infer scope from detection context.\"\"\"\n   141→    from .state_detector import IntroductionType\n   142→\n   143→    if detection.introduction_type == IntroductionType.SELF_ASSIGNMENT:\n   144→        return \"class-level\"\n   145→    return \"module-level\"\n   146→\n   147→\n   148→def _render_empty_section() -> str:\n   149→    return \"## Invariant Registry\\n\\nNo state variables detected.\\n\"\n   150→\n   151→\n   152→def _render_registry_section(\n   153→    entries: list[InvariantEntry],\n   154→    generated: list[Deliverable],\n   155→) -> str:\n   156→    \"\"\"Render Computational verbs (compute, extract, filter, etc.)\n    2. State mutation patterns (self._*, counter/offset/cursor)\n    3. Conditional logic patterns (guard, sentinel, flag, early return)\n\n    Negative signal suppression: doc-specific verbs (document, describe,\n    explain, list) suppress false positives on documentation deliverables.\n\n    Returns False for empty descriptions.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not description or not description.strip():\n        return False\n\n    lower = description.lower()\n\n    # Negative signal suppression: if doc verbs dominate, not behavioral\n    doc_signals = sum(1 for v in _DOC_VERBS if v in lower)\n    if doc_signals > 0:\n        # Check if any strong behavioral signal overrides\n        has_strong_behavioral = False\n        words = set(re.findall(r'\\b\\w+\\b', lower))\n        behavioral_verb_hits = words & _COMPUTATIONAL_VERBS\n        # Doc verbs win unless there are more behavioral signals\n        if len(behavioral_verb_hits) <= doc_signals:\n            return False\n        has_strong_behavioral = True\n\n    # Check computational verbs\n    words = set(re.findall(r'\\b\\w+\\b', lower))\n    if words & _COMPUTATIONAL_VERBS:\n        return True\n\n    # Check state mutation patterns\n    for pattern in _STATE_MUTATION_PATTERNS:\n        if re.search(pattern, lower):\n            return True\n\n    # Check conditional logic patterns\n    for pattern in _CONDITIONAL_PATTERNS:\n        if pattern in lower:\n            return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef decompose_deliverables(\n    deliverables: list[Deliverable],\n) -> list[Deliverable]:\n    \"\"\"Expand behavioral deliverables into Implement/Verify pairs.\n\n    For each behavioral deliverable D.x:\n    - desc_lower: str,\n) -> list[GuardState]:\n    \"\"\"Enumerate states for type change transitions.\"\"\"\n    if transition_kind == TypeTransitionKind.BOOL_TO_INT:\n        # Bool->int always has \"second enum state (maps to old false)\"),\n            ]),\n            GuardState(value=\"state_C\", semantic_meanings=[\n                SemanticMeaning(\"state_C\", \"new third state\"),\n            ]),\n        ]\n    elif transition_kind == TypeTransitionKind.ENUM_TO_STRING:\n        return [\n            GuardState(value=\"valid_string\", semantic_meanings=[\n                SemanticMeaning(\"valid_string\", \"matches expected enum name\"),\n            ]),\n            GuardState(value=\"empty_string\", semantic_meanings=[\n                SemanticMeaning(\"empty_string\", \"empty/missing value\"),\n            ]),\n            GuardState(value=\"unknown_string\", semantic_meanings=[\n                SemanticMeaning(\"unknown_string\", \"unrecognized value\"),\n            ]),\n        ]\n    return []\n\n\ndef _enumerate_guard_states(\n    var_name: str,\n    guard_kind: GuardKind,\n    desc_lower: str,\n) -> list[GuardState]:\n    \"\"\"Enumerate states for guard patterns based on kind.\"\"\"\n    if guard_kind == GuardKind.FLAG_CHECK:\n        # Boolean flags: true/false\n        if _matches_archetype(desc_lower, \"boolean\"):\n            return list(_KNOWN_ARCHETYPES[\"boolean\"])\n        return [\n            GuardState(value=\"true\", semantic_meanings=[\n                SemanticMeaning(\"true\", ]\n    elif guard_kind == GuardKind.SENTINEL_VALUE:\n        # Sentinel: has a special value + normal range\n        return [\n            GuardState(\n                value=\"sentinel\",\n **EARLY_RETURN**: `early return ... <var>`\n3. **SENTINEL_VALUE**: `<var> sentinel`, `sentinel for <var>`, `bounded by`, `threshold`\n4. **FLAG_CHECK**: `<var> guard`, `guard on/for <var>`, `<var> @property\n    def can_advance(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Pipeline can advance only if no blocking warnings exist.\"\"\"\n        return not self.has_blocking_warnings\n\n\ndef resolve_guards(\n owner\n\n    Non-ambiguous guards produce no deliverables and no warnings.\n    Suppressed guards produce no deliverables and no warnings.\n    \"\"\"\n    deliverables: list[Deliverable] = []\n    warnings: list[ReleaseGateWarning] = []\n    seq = 0\n\n    for detection in detections:\n        # Skip non-ambiguous guards\n        if not detection.has_ambiguity:\n            continue\n\n        # Skip suppressed guards\n        if detection.suppressed:\n            continue\n\n        # Generate guard_test deliverables\n        seq += 1\n\n        # 1. Semantic documentation deliverable\n        sem_doc = Deliverable(\n            id=f\"GT-{seq:04d}.sem\",\n            description=(\n                f\"Guard test: document every value of '{detection.guard_variable}' \"\n                f\"with its semantic meaning. \"\n                f\"States: {_format_states(detection)}\"\n            ),\n            kind=DeliverableKind.GUARD_TEST,\n            metadata={\n                \"guard_variable\": detection.guard_variable,\n                \"deliverable_id\": detection.deliverable_id,\n                \"test_type\": \"semantic_documentation\",\n            },\n        )\n        deliverables.append(sem_doc)\n\n        # 2. Uniqueness test deliverable\n        uniq_test = Deliverable(\n            id=f\"GT-{seq:04d}.uniq\",\n            description=(\n                f\"Guard test: verify each semantic state of '{detection.guard_variable}' \"\n                f\"maps to exactly one value. Type transition mapping (if applicable)\n        if detection.type_transition is not None:\n            trans_test = Deliverable(\n                id=f\"GT-{seq:04d}.trans\",\n                description=(\n                    f\"Guard test: verify all pre-transition semantic states of \"\n                    f\"'{detection.guard_variable}' ({detection.type_transition.value}) \"\n                    f\"have post-transition equivalents\"\n                ),\n                kind=DeliverableKind.GUARD_TEST,\n                metadata={\n                    \"guard_variable\": detection.guard_variable,\n                    \"deliverable_id\": detection.deliverable_id,\n                    \"test_type\": \"transition_mapping\",\n                    \"transition_kind\": detection.type_transition.value,\n                },\n            )\n            deliverables.append(trans_test)\n\n        #
